                               IF CostObjectFilter <> '' THEN
                                 SETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Code", CostObjectFilter);

                               IF ElementFilter <> '' THEN
                                 SETFILTER(Element, ElementFilter);

                                    SortKeyTransactions := 1;
                                  END;

                                  GetUnitCost("Job Ledger Entry", UnitCostJobLedgerEntry, TotalCostJobLedgerEntry);
                                END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF Job.GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', Job.TABLECAPTION, Job.GETFILTERS));
    END;

    PROCEDURE "*******"@1100285103();
    BEGIN
    END;

    PROCEDURE PopulateBuffer@1100285104(VAR ProjectRec@1100285100 : Record 11072003);
    VAR
      JobLedgerEntry@1100285101 : Record 11072005;
      CostObject@1100285102 : Record 1113;
      DimensionValue@1100285106 : Record 349;
      CurrYearFilter@1100285103 : Text[50];
      UnitCost@1100285105 : Decimal;
      TotalCost@1100285104 : Decimal;
    BEGIN

      // All transactions

      JobLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Job No.",Element,"Global Dimension 2 Code","Entry Type","Posting Date");
      IF Job."Single/Main/Sub Project" = Job."Single/Main/Sub Project"::"Main Project" THEN
        JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Main Project No.", Job."No.")
      ELSE
        JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Job No.", Job."No.");
      IF CostObjectFilter <> '' THEN
        JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Code", CostObjectFilter);
      IF ElementFilter <> '' THEN
        JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER(Element, ElementFilter);
      IF JobLedgerEntry.FINDSET(FALSE) THEN REPEAT
        CLEAR(TotalCost);
        IF UniversalBuffer.GET(JobLedgerEntry."Job No.", JobLedgerEntry."Global Dimension 2 Code") THEN BEGIN
            GetUnitCost(JobLedgerEntry, UnitCost, TotalCost);
            UniversalBuffer.Dec3 -= TotalCost + JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)";
            UniversalBuffer.MODIFY;
        END ELSE BEGIN
          GetUnitCost(JobLedgerEntry, UnitCost, TotalCost);
          UniversalBuffer.INIT;
          UniversalBuffer.Key1 := JobLedgerEntry."Job No.";
          UniversalBuffer.Key2 := JobLedgerEntry."Global Dimension 2 Code";
      //    UniversalBuffer.Text1 := FORMAT(JobLedgerEntry."Cost Type");
          IF JobLedgerEntry."Cost Type" = JobLedgerEntry."Cost Type"::Revenues THEN
            UniversalBuffer.Text1 := FORMAT(JobLedgerEntry."Cost Type")
          ELSE
            UniversalBuffer.Text1 := CostTypeText + ' ' + FORMAT(JobLedgerEntry."Cost Type");
          IF DimensionValue.GET(GLSetup."Global Dimension 2 Code", JobLedgerEntry."Global Dimension 2 Code") THEN
            UniversalBuffer.Text2 := DimensionValue.Name;

          //UniversalBuffer.Text2 := JobLedgerEntry.Description;
          UniversalBuffer.Dec3 -= TotalCost + JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)";
          IF JobLedgerEntry."Cost Type" = JobLedgerEntry."Cost Type"::Revenues THEN
            UniversalBuffer.Integer1 := 2
          ELSE
            UniversalBuffer.Integer1 := 1;
          UniversalBuffer.INSERT;
        END;

      UNTIL JobLedgerEntry.NEXT = 0;

      // Transactions in period
      CLEAR(JobLedgerEntry);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Job No.",Element,"Global Dimension 2 Code","Entry Type","Posting Date");
      IF Job."Single/Main/Sub Project" = Job."Single/Main/Sub Project"::"Main Project" THEN
        JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Main Project No.", Job."No.")
      ELSE
        JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Job No.", Job."No.");
      IF CostObjectFilter <> '' THEN
        JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Code", CostObjectFilter);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date", '%1..%2', StartDate, EndDate);
      IF ElementFilter <> '' THEN
        JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER(Element, ElementFilter);
      IF JobLedgerEntry.FINDSET(FALSE) THEN REPEAT
        IF UniversalBuffer.GET(JobLedgerEntry."Job No.", JobLedgerEntry."Global Dimension 2 Code") THEN BEGIN
            GetUnitCost(JobLedgerEntry, UnitCost, TotalCost);
            UniversalBuffer.Dec1 -= TotalCost + JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)";
            UniversalBuffer.MODIFY;
        END;
      UNTIL JobLedgerEntry.NEXT = 0;

      // Transactions current year
      CLEAR(JobLedgerEntry);
      //CurrYearFilter := FORMAT(CALCDATE('<-CY>', TODAY)) + '..';
      CurrYearFilter := FORMAT(CALCDATE('<-CY>', TODAY)) + '..' + FORMAT(EndDate);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Job No.",Element,"Global Dimension 2 Code","Entry Type","Posting Date");
      IF Job."Single/Main/Sub Project" = Job."Single/Main/Sub Project"::"Main Project" THEN
        JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Main Project No.", Job."No.")
      ELSE
        JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Job No.", Job."No.");
      IF CostObjectFilter <> '' THEN
        JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Code", CostObjectFilter);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date", CurrYearFilter);
      IF ElementFilter <> '' THEN
        JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER(Element, ElementFilter);
      IF JobLedgerEntry.FINDSET(FALSE) THEN REPEAT
        IF UniversalBuffer.GET(JobLedgerEntry."Job No.", JobLedgerEntry."Global Dimension 2 Code") THEN BEGIN
          GetUnitCost(JobLedgerEntry, UnitCost, TotalCost);
          UniversalBuffer.Dec2 -= TotalCost + JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)";
          UniversalBuffer.MODIFY;
        END;
      UNTIL JobLedgerEntry.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetUnitCost@1100285122(VAR JobLedgerEntry@1100285100 : Record 11072005;VAR UnitCost@1100285101 : Decimal;VAR TotalCost@1100285102 : Decimal);
    VAR
      CosObjecSalesPrice@1100285103 : Record 11020383;
    BEGIN
      IF JobLedgerEntry."Cost Type" = JobLedgerEntry."Cost Type"::Labor THEN BEGIN
        CASE UnitCostOption OF
          UnitCostOption::"Standard Cost":
          BEGIN
            UnitCost := JobLedgerEntry."Unit Cost (LCY)";
            TotalCost := JobLedgerEntry."Total Cost (LCY)";
          END;

          UnitCostOption::"Sales Price":
          BEGIN
            CosObjecSalesPrice.RESET;
            CosObjecSalesPrice.SETRANGE("Project No.", JobLedgerEntry."Job No.");
            CosObjecSalesPrice.SETRANGE("Cost Object", JobLedgerEntry."Global Dimension 2 Code");
        //    CosObjecSalesPrice.SETRANGE("Ending Date"
            IF CosObjecSalesPrice.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
              UnitCost := CosObjecSalesPrice."Sales Price";
              TotalCost := CosObjecSalesPrice."Sales Price" * JobLedgerEntry.Quantity;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              UnitCost := JobLedgerEntry."Unit Cost (LCY)";
              TotalCost := JobLedgerEntry."Total Cost (LCY)";
            END;
          END;
        END;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        UnitCost := JobLedgerEntry."Unit Cost (LCY)";
        TotalCost := JobLedgerEntry."Total Cost (LCY)";
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      140526 ITERO.DJ added captions to multiple fields
      140603 ITERO.DJ changed number formatting to achieve better spacing

      140711 ITERO.GH IME-168 Changed Label Progress1Caption
      140715 ITERO.GH IME165 Report CaptionML SE and NO added
      150908 ITERO.MK RFC-022 Copy of report Financial Overview Oriject, with adjustments
      151020 CLP Adjusted filtering in function GetPrognosisRevenue.


      Om huvudprojekt h„mta fr†n underprojekten
      Kolla ”ver f„lten i transaktionsdetaljer
      Kolla filter
      160415 ITERO.PEPF Company name from table "Company Information"
    }
    END.

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
